O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three sons, I have fulfilled this book that is beyond the science of medicine, and has gathered its fulfillment in it, and has ended through its exposures and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to my vision that I have fulfilled this with the treatment, which is from the work of hands, which is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is forbidden in our region and is despised in every way, if it is perceived by the science and craft, and there is nothing more to do than the small descriptions in books written by the ancients that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And this has led to the error and vanity, and the intentions are closed and the science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation; et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	I seem to think that I will revive it together with the arrangement of this cauterization according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation; and I will bring together the forms of the cauterizers and other instruments of the work with the adjustment of the declaration and preparation of it, as it is their craft.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no one can find a master of hands in our time, the art of medicine is elongated.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And he who enters into the science of anatomy, as Galen says, must know the judgment of the bones, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of parts, and have knowledge of the bones, nerves, and joints, and the number of limbs, and the brain and the number of eyes, and the movement and rest of the limbs, and the issue of the same.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc; et meismement en l’art de main.	And for this reason, Iocras says that the non is not with the non, and with the will is little; and at the same time in the art of hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes; ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	In the introduction of this book, we say that who is not acquainted with the things that are said, if he does not err and does not confuse the men; therefore, I have often seen these who become entangled in this science and then abandon it and senselessness and experiment.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col; por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	For I see a foolish man who covers his head with scrophules or the neck of a woman, and covers the arteries of the neck; because so much blood issues outside that the woman dies in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans; si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	And see if another matter that treats a piercing of an old man's ear, and the piercing was large; if it is carried out with it, along with a piece of the bladder, and he died in the third year.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I have already been accused of the treatment, and see the position of the assistant and the size of the piercing, and if it was not cut well, he died.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie; et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine; et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie; et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	And see if another matter that treated the leg of our king who had a broken bone, and with the splint it was on the wound; and the patients who were ignorant were forced to break the bone on the wound as soon as possible, and did not leave any pain in the wound, and left it finally; and he commanded that he should not be disturbed; and later, when the leg was all frozen and the bone and came to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe; et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	I am called to come to him, and I hurried to come limb by limb; and when I loosened it if it was in pain and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner; et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	But all paths of the corruption were already confirmed or member, and could not be healed; and the corruption continued to spread through the member as long as the member was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And see another mirror that will fall and be enchanted, and then inflamed by the malice of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For chancre, when it is free from melancholic matter, only then does one dare to touch it with iron if it is not part of the limb that can heal what is corrupt.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions: c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions; et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	And for this reason, three-year-old children, you should know that the work of hands is divided into two parts: it is knowledge, whether or not it is dangerous in other arrangements; and I will show you in each chapter of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez; et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit; et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	And for this reason, you should know that the work of hands is divided into two parts: it is knowledge, whether or not it is dangerous in other arrangements; and I will show you in each chapter of this book where there is fear and danger. If you keep your children away from evil, they will not be able to speak ill of you. Take your weapons in hand, and use them lightly but firmly, and use the best way possible for the grace of God, so that you may come to salvation and be healthy; and let go of the unpleasant diseases of grief; and keep your weapons from doing harm, and have faith in yourself so that you can come from this world to another of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens: «Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Gall's admonishes from his warnings: "Do not take medicine for sick people, lest you be called murderers.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have heard this treated in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez; et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	The first chapter is about fire cauterization and medicinal cauterization, and it is the first chapter of the book that deals with the head up to the feet; as well as the forms of strums, stitches, and all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses; et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	The second chapter is about cutting and piercing, as well as ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things; and it is the chapter ordered and the forms of strums.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses; et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things; and it is ordered by the hands of the chief surgeons, and the forms of the stitches.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, let us remember our work, and it is necessary that I give the quality of the help and not every complexity.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus; et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu; et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	I say that the quality of the help and not every complexity is the longest word and subtle science and the secret remedy; and for this they speak more of the wounds, and agree with each other, and few words they have to say, because I doubt the longevity.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions: c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	I say that burning helps universally with all complexions, provided they have matter. This is to know the complexion hot in matter, and the complexion dry in matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide; et li autre dirent le contraire: que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	In hot and dry complexions, no one prescribes it and says that burning is very helpful; the other says the opposite: that burning is only useful for diseases that come from chlorosis and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour; et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	For the nature of fire is hot, and it should not be used for hot diseases caused by chlorosis or dryness; but those who say the opposite that burning is very helpful for hot diseases that come from the hearts of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you perceive the heart of the chest and its moisture at the complexion of hot fire, you touch the heart cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I accommodate to this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it once by experiment.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens; des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	And all ways, it does not interfere more than he who has experienced it and knows by long use of the cauterization chapter, and the diversity of complexions of men, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and their occurrences and spasms; other complexions have no fear, yet in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And they are designed to resemble and correspond to the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, children, that cauterization with fire is the best of all remedies, and more beneficial than burning medicines.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fire is simple, and only brings harm to the member that is burned, and does not harm other members.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation; et par aventure ocit lou malaide Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The burning medicines come from one member to another by removing, and bring the diseases of grief to health; and by chance, the patient should use the fire for its high quality and the goodness of its substance, not because it causes harm, if it does not have excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses; et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant; or le recevez en vos pensees.	1. And I found this in my research through experiment and the length of service and the study I have given to the art, and it is true about things; and for this I excuse the length of the word, because I only want to reveal to you the secret that is inside or fire, and the quality of the work, as it treats the diseases of the body, just as the philosopher says in demonstrating; and you should receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	2. And know, son, that the burns are made in accordance with what is appropriate for the size of the skin.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere; et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	3. And I say that cauterization is allowable in all sizes, because the wounds are not misplaced by the help of cauterization; and moreover, if the cauterization is for necessary pains and hurts that cannot wait for the size that greatest malice comes to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire; car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue; et il le dient ensi; mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	1. And do not think otherwise, it is a thin hair, as the wise man does; for the disease that is cured by cauterization has no return; and he says thus; but it is not so if one takes care, because cauteries are only a medicine that dries the complexion, and drys the humors that cause pain, and is worthy of medicine for its courage, and for its virtue in its work and its ladyship.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut; et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie; mais ce avient poc.	2. And it is true that the disease never returns according to the complexion of the patient and the nature of the disease, and they are assembled in him by the acquisition of flesh and the superfluities of things, unless cauteries are administered to him or he has little excess and moisture, like cauteries for pain, and the superfluities, and only a part of the pain returns; but this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir; mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	1. And many people do not understand that cauterization is a part of medicine, and this can be seen; but they only believe that cauterization is after medicine, but we understand it is false, and cauterization is part of medicine because when we administer remedies for any disease and they are ineffective, then we use cauterization, and it is effective.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	2. Therefore, it is well that cauterization is part of medicine, but not according to the attention of foolish people.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance; et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes; et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	3. The ancients said that a gold cauterization instrument was as harmful as one made of iron, and they said this because of the quality of the gold and its high substance; and they said that gold cauterization did not cause any harm, but it is true that it does, and I have experienced this in some people; and gold cauterization is as good as iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez; et s’on le chaufe trop; si font au feu; et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	When you wield an instrument of gold, you do not know its true color until it is heated by the color of the gold, and it has cooled; and if it is heated too much, it melts; then it has enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that is why we use fire cauteries in our work, which we have found effective.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or you have ordered this chapter of the sharp tools, because it is more easily found.
dou cautere olivaire	oil cauteries
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cauterization is effective against moisture and cold in the head, and it is done by the cause of a disease called "soda", and by the cause of many humors that descend from the sharp tools to the ears, eyes, and numerous dreams and toothache and throat pain, and also for all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, stroke, and apoplexy, and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir; et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	The form of this cauterization is that if the surgeon is purged by a solvent medicine modifying the third or fourth degree, according to what the virtues and the age and the accustomed use of the surgeon can endure; and then cut off the surgeon's own chief.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis; aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz; et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And then make it stand between your hands, and press them together; afterwards place the root of your palm tree on the root of his finger between his two fingers; and if you see your two means, if he bleeds from the cut, wash the cauterization which is called "olivare", of which the form is:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant; puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit; et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit; aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors; aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre; et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	The first sentence to translate is: "And place the lesion with ink on it, and make descending and pulling your hand little by little until you see the bone; if you don't see it, continue the cauterization as long as you see the bone just like I told you; then take a piece of linen, and wet it with water, and put it on the lesion, and let it stay for three days; then put on a moist cloth on a bandage; and leave it until the burn is healed; then cure the wound with the ointment called 'tetrafarmaçon' as long as it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge; et por ce si aide mues.	And if the old ones say that as the wound becomes more overgrown, it more purges itself; and therefore it helps to aid.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of them say that one must shave the cauterization so much that part of the bone is exposed, and then remove what is diseased bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors; et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte; aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	And they say that the cauterization must be shaved so much that it is as wide as the vagina of a woman, and as deep as the fist of a man, because the humors flow out; and then it must be treated for a long time overgrown; afterward it must be cured and seared.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor; et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier; car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres; et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	1. These two methods of cauterization do not seem to be the best in any way, despite any fear one may have; and I seem to think that I should leave them; for the head of the shoulder is often weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we have seen in other parts of the body; and even when the patient's strength is weak naturally, the first appearance of cauterization seems more salve and milder to me, and therefore I use it accordingly.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	1. of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres; et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	1. When the entire head is in chronic pain and lasts for a long time, if it must use the drugs called "cochie" and pills, as well as purging of the head and oils and plasters; and when the cauterization is done as we have said before, and it does not work.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit; adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	The patient's head wound is of great nature and should not be too deep; therefore, we cauterize with the fire cautery a small area as we have mentioned earlier.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»; et est I leus en coi on met ventouses; et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os: li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors; et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	After cauterizing each corne of the eye, as we have previously described, and then cauterizing the area called "vessels"; and these are the ones where you put in a ventouse; and hold your hand so that you do not see too much of the bone: the patient feels too much pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will explain further; and it is necessary that the cauterizations of the eyes be more superficial than those of the chin, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	A burn cauterization of the head
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie: adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	In one part of the head, sudden pain occurs, and it spreads throughout the disease, and the head is purged with medicines modified, and the other treatments I mentioned in the division of diseases were made, but none of them helped: therefore, I performed cauterization in two ways, that is, with hot and cold medicine.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir; et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres; et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III; puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	If you apply a poultice of alum with hot medicine, and it draws out the puss and the wound closes within two hours, then make a temple over the painful part so that you can pour the alum poultice on it; when it is poured, let the person lie down and hold the wound for twelve hours; then remove the poultice and apply a plaster of egg yolk to the wound, leaving it on for two or three days; then dip your hand in cold water as long as it is possible.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	After the application of ointment when it is healthy; and if you see that there are no such medicines as I have written or treated of in my book on medicines that cause vomiting.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The iron burn if it follows this method.

de la cure de fistule par cautere	The treatment of fistulas by burning

Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cauterization at the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors; aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers; et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	If not, then continue the cauterization again once more, and if you have experience with it, and leave it for three days; after that, put cotton wool on the dressing, and apply the desiccant ointment as much as it is dry, and when 40 hours have passed and it is dry, if you put an acidic corrosive medicine on it so that the bone is exposed, then follow what comes in your chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing fistulas that no ancient ones mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu; aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Understands the fistula, and then puts in the furnace the subtlest candle of which is the form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc; et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil; et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe: li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	And they make it to the quantity of one .З. of plunk; and hold your hand firmly, and do not move the patient's arm at all, until the plunks melt and flow to their oil; and it is necessary to put on the oiled cotton cloth in the abin of uefz or in awe: the plunk if it is well for the fistula, and the healthy for the health.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the fire cautery we have described, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then it is necessary to administer purgatives to the child, and bring the fistula back to its proper place according to what is best for the child's own health.
des crevaices en levres	cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Often there are cracks in the lips that are called "cracks," and also in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have described in divisions, and the cure does not work, then use a small fire cautery according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font; aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And place the patient in those cracks as much as possible; afterwards, heal the limb by making it healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the gall
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule; et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie: adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule; aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu; et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez; et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	When an abscess comes from the gallbladder or uterus, or fallopian tube, or teeth, and it becomes inflamed and forms a fistule; and you treat it as we have said in divisions, and it does not benefit much: therefore, it is necessary that you cauterize according to the size of the fistule; after the bolt or rupture of the fistule, and hold your hand until the fire reaches the font of the limb, and if it goes in; and make once or twice, after the treatment we have said in the treatments, as long as it is healthy; and if it is cured once or twice, it is good; and if not, it is necessary to expose the limb and open the corrupt bone, according to what you will find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	The first sentence to translate is: "Ou cautere
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain; aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent; et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent; aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit; aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat them with medicine and it does not work, then put a poultice of malarial ointment on your gum; afterward, wash the cauterization that formed afterwards in this way, as if you were putting a collar around the root of the tooth; then tighten your hand and continue the cauterization according to your will; after filling the mouth with bitter-tasting ointment, paint it once an hour and rinse it thoroughly.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	1. And in part, the teeth that were moving are confirmed, and the gums become soft and restrained, and the moisture becomes dry.
de la dolor des dens	2. of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres: et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	3. When the pain of the teeth comes from cold, or it is cold, and the remedies of medicine do not help, then it has a duty to cauterize in two ways: and cauterization by burning and cauterization by fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain; aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez; et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	4. If cauterization by burning is such that you use sheep fat and put it in a copper or iron spoon; then take cotton and wrap it around the tip of a needle, and make the painful tooth hot, and hold it until it cools down; and often I do this until the virtue reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that the wool and cotton are burning in the fire, and put the painful tooth on the iron, and make it hot until the fat reaches the end of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide; aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez; fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	1. If the fire cautery is large enough to burn a piece of iron or lead, and it is quite big that the smoke does not reach the patient's mouth; then heat the cautery, and form it according to this, and place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery is cool; do this often as the pain will be less for you or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	2. And it is necessary that the patient fills their mouth with hot water in the pressure of this cautery, and then it will cool down; and this is the form of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir; et c’est li forme de la caine:	I make a cut according to what you want, and according to the size you have; this is the shape of the knife:
des scrophules	of scrophules
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie; et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume; et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors; et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee; aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the scrophules are fleshy and cold, and do not respond to digestion with medicines, then wash the knife's edge with water after it comes out of forming, and make two openings for the fumes to escape from the other side; and put the knife's edge on the abscess once, or as it may be, until it reaches the font of the abscess; and if the abscess is small, then put the knife according to the amount of the abscess, and leave it for three days; and wrap the wound with soft cloth as the wound oozes; after curing the wound with ointments and plasters as it is healthy.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the collar:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives; aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	When the moistors win against the hard bones, and at the same time when the cold complexion comes, it is then necessary that the patient be treated first with soluble medicines; after that, I perform the fire cautery at the root of the throat, and make sure you do not come too close to the throat, and do not burn the skin but only a little.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant; et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, I perform another cautery at the joint of the dole col at the head of the spine, and it is called "clavile" as we have before; and cure the limb as we have said until it is healthy.
de la toust	The first sentence to translate is: "Ou c
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai ij cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis; et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles; et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	When all diseases of the face are caused by cold moisture, and the patient has no fever or chill, and it is an old disease, then make cauterizations at the places you wish; and the other cauterization is between the two eyes; and that cauterization called "clavicle" is according to the form mentioned earlier.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles; et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	And if you see, make cauterizations by pricking all the cauterizations called "points" in the form mentioned earlier for the disease of the ears; and let the points be as close as possible, or farther.
Aprés cure le leu selonc ceu qui est devant dit, et soit li cauteres a III rains selonc ceste forme:	After treating the wound according to what has been said, and if it is a burn, then apply cauterization with three rains according to this form:
Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And because they are lighter, because you make three in one.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder.
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit; aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre; et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	After if you have shaved the beard on his back and on his chest; after softening the skin that was tightened by the titillation as it was with your left hand; and if the joint is dislocated, then cauterize the area with two ners douqueil like this form:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres; et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres; et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	1. And cauterize the loaf as much as it pierces the costal side, and it would come from the future sharp cauterization of four cauterizations; and this is done with the cauterization tool that has three needles, because the appearance of cauterization is six cauterizations; and the needles are according to the subtlety of a tent and it is the form of the future sharp cauterization that has three needles:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	2. And no time is ever adjusted on this one nerve because it has eight cauterizations:
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil; aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	3. After place the cauterization tool on the wound with silk; after let the patient rest, and do not pull on the limbs as much as they are well relaxed:
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	If it is dislocated, something comes out quickly, so a cauterization is made on the large cauterization clavicle, or rather, a cauterization is made by pinching.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and it is dried by the moisture and is healthy for the patient.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When cold sweats and moisture come to the stomach as it is drawn towards its complexion, and the purges are multiplied to him, and the customary cures are applied, and he does not benefit, then it is necessary that the patient be sewn on his back, and his legs and hands extended.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture; et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	1. For this reason, I made three burns on the leg of the horse for the quantity of a doe, at all the cauterization points, and two burns to soften the two costals so that the cauterizations are at three angles, and there should be space between them as they will separate when they start to sweat; and they should be cauterizations so that they turn purple in the two parts of the neck, and the figure of the cauterizations should be according to this form without any deviation.
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	2. And if you see a large burn on the stomach according to this form; and the one who suffers from this burn, should cauterize by touching and holding the stomach at the point where you saw the quantity; then the cauterization should be on all the points called "points".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure of the cure we had before, as long as it is healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez; et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil; et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient; et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi; et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere; et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez; et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais; et c’est li forme:	After the liver suffers from pain and moisture, as long as it is healthy due to its natural complexion; and the patient is treated according to what we have said in divisions, and if it does not benefit him, then the patient should be burned with cauteries according to this form and this figure and this quantity on the liver, defending the gallbladder, whether the bile from the liver comes; and there should be space between each cauterization of a groove in the liver; and they should be long enough to cover the entire cautery; and it should only be one half of the knee, and it should press with the hand on both sides of the cauterization; and if it cannot, then it should be gently extended and lifted, and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors; et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	If you wish, if you burn these sharp cauteries, be subtle and gentle in the art, and be careful not to burn all of the skin, for you will dry out the entire body; and that it does not become soggy, because the hair is very delicate in one place and the skin is sensitive to touch.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile: s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort; et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	If it has entered the liver, and you see whether it is in the liver or on the skin: if it is in the liver, it feels great pain but not too much; and if it is on the skin, it feels sharp pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste; et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	And when this cure is done, if the hair is shaved on the head; and then stretch the limb or the affected part, and then heat the cauterization that is similar to the wound, according to what form it is.
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	1. And cauterize as much as the hair is long, and it grows back slowly, until the poultice is all used up; after the cure according to the cure of wounds as soon as it is healthy; and only this cauterization uses no other hands but those who have studied for a long time in the art of medicine, and by these hands these diseases have never been corrupted once.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	2. And can it be overcome with great effort, and it seems to me that it is better to leave it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	3. Of cold cauterization
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere: pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois; et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe; et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc; et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules; et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	4. The ancients said that one must make cold cauterization using roots of Aristolochia, and in this manner: take a root of Aristolochia as long as you can find it, and it should be dry, and it should be large and long as your two; and the oil, and you heat it, and cauterize as much as possible between the force and the col, and make two punctures on descending in the part that is rough like the beard; and make two punctures between the fifth costal and the sixth, descending from the neck; and make a puncture in the pis, and the other in the stomach, and in the spines, and let the cautery between the spines deflower; and do not press too hard with your hand, as you would smell.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And no ancient one has ever said that no man uses a fire cautery like the scalpel, and they thrust it between the ribs, as soon as it reaches the abscess; and then there is the pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	However, in this case, there is pain or the patient has already died, or an abscess has formed that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse that we have described, and it does not benefit, therefore there are three ways to cauterize that you know.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	1. If you are doing three or four cauterizations, do them according to the length of the hairs, following the figure of the cauterization we have described before; and do not press too hard with your hand on all the cauterization, and let the patient's arm be near his back; and another way of cauterization is if you scrape the cauterization that has two needles, as we have shown it in the dislocation of the shoulder; and ease the knee which is where the hairs are, or the pain from the wound comes from the side, and make the elevations of the knee according to the knee, according to the length of the chest, and the cauterization should be according to the width of the chest.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After burning the two nerves until the pain is felt from the other side, then take the cauterization tool, and then insert it into the fire cautery at three points. If you see, cauterize all the way to the cauterization tool at four points.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has gotten wet with long tents, and this is enough that the other cures before say.
de ydropisie	of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not good for dropsy, for it is done in the way called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat according to the ways we have said in divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four caustizations entor the bowels, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the gallbladder, and two on the back near the spine, and one at the anus; and make sure the cauterization is close to the spine of the knee.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After the cauterization, let the patient have loose, long hair, and do not delay the treatment of the physician after the cauterization; healing will come quickly, and the two interpretations will be assembled with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cauterization is made on the belly with the clavicle that we show before; and on the back it is olive-colored, according to what is shown before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the enflaming of the wounds
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the wounds are enflamed by hydration, and are plain green, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the wound between the auricle and the anus; and gently place your hand with the cauterization so as not to return.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too far into the flesh, otherwise it will cause more harm than good. The cauterization should be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Afterward, make two cauterizations on each leg at the pointed end of the thigh; and make one cut through the flesh in front and the other towards the back, passing through the leg; and leave the cauterizations exposed to cure for as long as necessary, according to the patient's condition; after which, apply the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the mustard
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the stomach comes from cold and moisture, as long as the virtuous and digestive substances that are in the stomach and intestine are swollen and cannot be cured by usual methods; and you see the patient very suffering and of great vertut, if make I grand cauterization on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before or on the small intestine, at the cauterization circle; and IV cauterizations are made subtle at all the small cauterizations clavile, and II cauterizations on the hams.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see many moistures and the patient suffers, then perform a fire cautery on the point, and a cautery on each side, and two cauteries on the stomach of the large intestine because the cure is beneficial when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	If the hemorrhoids are fund or one or more, and they are old and large, full of cold, moist, corrupted humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not profit, then make cauterizations: III on the spine of the back, which is all deflated and deflated in triangulating, and a cauterization on the bowel II doses; and if you think that the stomach is cold, and the meat is not cooked, and the face swells, then the face on the large cauterization on the stomach, as it is said before, and the other on the liver, and the other on the gallbladder at all the cauterizations; and leave the cauterization over long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing the limb as much as possible.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the chondrosarcoma which is called "thelul

When you remove the carbuncle, if the cauterizing instrument seems too hot, and then place it all over the carbuncle; and leave as much of your hand as the cauterant reaches to the vein's birth, without cutting; do this once or twice, and if it has pain from the carbuncle, cauterize each time as we have said; after the cure of wounds as much as possible; and if you cauterize with a large cauterizing instrument, it will give more help.
de plaie mal curee	Of a wound that was not properly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear tightening or opening, we will tell you in his own words if there is any illness that cannot be healed by burning.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it is awake and produces watery and corrupted excrement, if you provide it with enough food, and make sure to keep the whole tent intact, as much as possible.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After the burning is done, and the wound is rased, and the boute is pulled out according to the amount of food that entered, and the cautery is resumed as soon as the corss and corrupted parts are clean and healed, once or twice, depending on the amount of blood loss; and the patient is given an injection of le nerf which is available, and large doses.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	1. If the fistula is in the course of the ureter and intestine, and it is not removed, and one does not perform this surgery, and thinks that it is not a serious matter; after healing the wound until it is healthy, if the fistula is still there, and the materials are long tens, then it is certain that the wound is completely healed; and if the materials are not long, then it is certain that the wound is not completely healed, and the bone at the site is corrupted. And so, one of these that we will say in his wound.
de la maladie des reins	2. of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide. de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is full and weak from the head and moisture, if the patient retains urine, then cauterize in the part of the bladder where the urethra enters, either on the left or right side, and make each cauterization as long as one of your thumbs; and also cauterize the back of the bladder, or two if you wish; and make the cauterizations according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the marriages
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the wife is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flow is corrupted and comes late; and when they come, it causes great pain: therefore, it is necessary to apply three cauteries along the thigh, as we have said or cauterization of the bladder, and second cauterization of the back; and if it is a clamp, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the thigh, and for this reason if it does not move from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the knees are in a different department than desired, then it comes that you cauterize the patient's shoulder above the thigh at the cauterization like a circle, and point before the knee on the thigh as it turns, if the thigh is in the circle; and if it is a cauterization like those we have cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, make three olive-sized cauterizations and they should be as large as all the hairs; and the cure will be fine once it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the shoulder
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the shoulder joint, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is cured as we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: therefore, you must purge the patient of large humors of fetid pills or other bones-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the manner of cauterization is according to two methods: it means to assemble burning medicines and cauterize with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	The fire cautery is done according to these methods, and some are like this: you cauterize at the end of the hair where there are three triangular cautery marks according to this form, and make a deep and large hole between each cauterization point of a hair, and it should be olive oil; never cauterize on the edge of the hair, because there are four according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, that the cauterization is done at the circle we have mentioned in the dislocation of the hair; but do it in a way that the circles contain the entire hair, and all its points are equal.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And that is how it is done in sciatica, when the pain holds in the hip, and does not reach the thigh or the knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And when the pain reaches the thigh and the knee, one should cauterize there either the ankle or the malleolus, on the side where there is less flesh; and whether it is cutaneous or subcutaneous, and whether the patient feels that the pain extends to two points or close to it, one should cauterize at the point where they feel the pain three or four times, which is called "points.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain persists, make it a cauterization; and if the pain is in the groin towards the thigh, make it a fire cautery or circular one, and take good care of all your cauterizations that you do not burn the nerves and the large arteries, and that you do not cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen others who have cauterized on the ankle, and they burned so much that the entire leg became inflamed, and the foot as well, and it was noticed and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of the stomach where he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	If the pain is in two parts assembled, make a fire cautery on both sides according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the sage said in the fire cautery of the shoulder, if it is like this, make the iron as follows: make one piece and so it is big like some giant's nail or a smaller one, and it should be interwoven and it should be between interweaves and it should be spaced out like a piece of wire; and they should be interwoven in two parts and they should also be like noses, and it should have a good handle; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	1. And let it be washed as many times as it is all red and glistening, and then put on the handle of the malady's cauterizing tool, and make it curve once around the cauterized area; and leave it for three days; and then apply ointment, and leave the wound open for long tens; after the cure of the ointment, as it becomes healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	1. Albucasim says that we use little of this cautery due to its fear of the pain of the patient, and if we see little use; and all this is burns, which can be endured, and it or it does not hurt.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The first line of the text translates to: "If you have a fire cautery and an instrument for interlocking in your hand descends the edge of the door, and is either of iron or of brass with a long handle, and in the upper part it has II of us, and between each of them the quantity of a doe; and they are overturned and separated, and join together according to this form:".
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After you place the handle of the axe in the patient's hand gripping it firmly, and press your hand down on the handle; after heating the two circles of the hot awl that has been heated in the fire, and leaves it for an hour, and suffers the patient's pain and the shock of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For the fire cautery, it is similar to burning; and when the burning has been done, one should hold the hand with the instrument and gently raise the hair of the affected area, and leave it for three days, and apply as much ointment as there is blackness in the bandage; and then leave it for three days that it may become straight; and this will help after the cure of wounds as soon as it is healthy.
